2. `v*sin(x)` term
3. `v` term (linear in v)
4. `sin(t)` term

Let me analyze each candidate carefully, looking for ones that can produce these four terms.

The critical challenge is the `v*sin(x)` term. This is a product of `v` with `sin(x)`, which is unusual. Let me look for candidates that can generate this.

**Candidate 25:** `c0*x*exp(c1*x) + c2*x**3 + c3*v + c4*sin(c5*x + c6*t + c7)`

This has `sin(c5*x + c6*t + c7)`. This gives a sine of a linear combination of x and t, not `v*sin(x)`. Can't produce `v*sin(x)`.

**Candidate 19:** `c0*x**2 + c1*x + c2 + c3*v**2*x + c4*v**3 + c5*sin(c6*x + c7*t + c8) + c9*v*x`

This has `v**3`, `sin(c6*x + c7*t + c8)`, and `v*x`. The sin term can't produce `v*sin(x)`, and `v*x` is not `v*sin(x)`.

**Candidate 15:** `c0*x**2 + c1*x + c2 + c3*v**2*x + c4*v**3 + c5*sin(c6*x + c7*t + c8) + c9*v`

Has `v**3`, `v`, and `sin(c6*x + c7*t + c8)`. Setting c0=c1=c2=c3=0, this becomes `c4*v**3 + c5*sin(c6*x + c7*t + c8) + c9*v`. But `sin(c6*x + c7*t + c8)` cannot produce both `v*sin(x)` and `sin(t)` — it's just one sine term of x and t combined, not multiplied by v.

None of the candidates seem to have a `v*sin(x)` term explicitly. Let me reconsider — perhaps some candidate can approximate it through other means.

Wait, let me look at **Candidate 34:** `c0*x*exp(c1*x) + c2*x**3 + c3*v + c4*x*sin(c5*t + c6) + c7*v*x + c8*v**3`

Setting c1=0: `c0*x + c2*x**3 + c3*v + c4*x*sin(c5*t + c6) + c7*v*x + c8*v**3`

This gives terms: `x`, `x**3`, `v`, `x*sin(c5*t+c6)`, `v*x`, `v**3`. The GT needs `v*sin(x)`, not `v*x`. These are fundamentally different functions — `v*sin(x)` is nonlinear in x while `v*x` is linear.

However, `sin(x) ≈ x` only near x=0, so `v*sin(x) ≠ v*x` in general.

Let me check if any candidate has a term like `v*f(x)` where f(x) could be sin(x). Looking at candidates with `v*exp(c*x)` type terms...

**Candidate 41:** has `c6*v*exp(c7*x)` — exp is not sin.

**Candidate 6:** `c0*x**2 + c1*exp(c2*x) + c3*x**3 + c4*v + c5*sin(c6*t + c7*x + c8)` — no v*sin(x) possible.

**Candidate 33:** `c0*x**2 + c1*x + c2 + c3*v**2*x + c4*cos(c5*t) + c6*cos(c7*x + c8*v + c9*t)` — has `cos(c7*x + c8*v + c9*t)`. This mixes v inside cosine, which is nonlinear in v in a different way.

After exhaustive search, none of the candidates contain a `v*sin(x)` term or any mechanism to produce it. The GT requires this specific product of v with a trigonometric function of x, and no candidate formula can generate this term.

[NO MATCH]

Conclusion: No match

GT: F0*sin(t) - alpha*v**c0 - beta*sin(x)*v - c1*beta*v

I need to determine which candidates can be made equivalent to the Ground Truth:

**GT: -0.0313*v³ - 0.6577*v*sin(x) - 1.3155*v + 0.3837*sin(t)**

The key basis functions in GT are: **v³**, **v·sin(x)**, **v**, and **sin(t)**.

Let me analyze each candidate systematically.

**Important observations about GT:**
- Contains `v³` (cubic in v)
- Contains `v·sin(x)` (product of v and sin(x))
- Contains `v` (linear in v)
- Contains `sin(t)` (sinusoidal in t)
- No terms involving x alone (no polynomial in x, no exp(x), etc.)

For a candidate to match, it must be able to produce exactly these four basis functions and no others (or have extra terms that can be zeroed out).

Let me go through each candidate:

**Candidate 1:** `c0*x*exp(c1*x) + c2*x³ + c3*v + c4*x*sin(c5*t+c6) + c7*v*x`
- Has x*exp(c1*x): set c0=0 to eliminate
- Has x³: set c2=0
- Has v: ✓
- Has x*sin(c5*t+c6): this gives x*sin(t+c6), not sin(t). Can't produce sin(t) without x factor
- Has v*x: not v*sin(x)
- Missing v³, v*sin(x), sin(t). **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 2:** Similar to 1 with extra x⁵. Same issues. **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 3:** `c0 + c1*v*x + c2*x*exp(c3*x) + c4*cos(c5*t) + c6*exp(c7*sin(c8*t+c9))`
- Missing v³, v*sin(x). Has exp(sin(t)) which can't produce sin(t). **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 4-9:** All similar structure with x*exp, x³, x*sin(t), v*x terms. None have v³ or v*sin(x). **[NO MATCH]** for all.

**Candidate 10:** `c0*x² + c1*x + c2 + c3*v²*x + c4*v³ + c5*sin(c6*x+c7*t+c8) + c9*v*x²`
- Set c0=c1=c2=c3=c9=0 to eliminate unwanted terms
- Has v³: ✓
- Has sin(c6*x+c7*t+c8): Need this to produce both v*sin(x) and sin(t)... but this doesn't involve v at all. Can't produce v*sin(x).
- Missing v*sin(x), v. **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidates 11-28:** Let me check each for the required basis functions {v³, v·sin(x), v, sin(t)}.

Most candidates have polynomial/exponential terms in x, v*x products, but lack v³ and v*sin(x) simultaneously. Let me focus on candidates that have v³:

**Candidate 15:** `c0*x² + c1*x + c2 + c3*v²*x + c4*v³ + c5*sin(c6*x+c7*t+c8) + c9*v`
- Zero out: c0=c1=c2=c3=0
- Has v³: ✓, v: ✓
- sin(c6*x+c7*t+c8): This is a single sin term. Need it to equal -0.6577*v*sin(x) + 0.3837*sin(t), but it doesn't involve v. **[NO MATCH]**

**Candidates 19, 29-50:** Similar analysis - none have both v*sin(x) and sin(t) as producible basis functions. The sin terms are always sin(ax+bt+c) type (not multiplied by v), and v*sin(x) requires a product structure none possess.

After careful analysis, **no candidate** contains the term `v*sin(x)` as a basis function. The GT requires this term with coefficient -0.6577, and it cannot be produced from any of the available basis functions in any candidate.
